My son and daughter have been training  for just under one year at POL. They train five days a week most of the time and  have improved significantly. < Text>
I just moved to El Cajon from "the Central Coast" (north of Santa Barbara...).  Well I ordered a chicken [shredded not grilled] burrito + rice & beans on the inside of my burrito + wet with green sauce (mojado verde).  It tastes GREAT!--Very flavorful...
Also, I think the prices are just right.  Where I used to live, (about 300 miles north of here) the same burrito would've cost the same price--but the size & quality were both not as good..
They got my order right the first time too.
So far, so good--in my humble opinion. (I'm
a fairly picky person by the way).
Maybe I got lucky (based on some of the reviews that I read), but I think they deserve a lot better than a 3.6 star rating!
It's been my favorite shredded chicken burrito in the area in the 2-3 months that I've been here!
Nuff said.</Text>

< review>
First time going to Los Panchos , I asked vegetarian burrito.
The woman working at the time confirmed it was a vegetarian burrito.
Once I was home I obviously bit the burrito a couple times and taste something weird but since I didn't grow up eating pig lard I didn't think anything of it but since it tastes different, I called Los Panchos  and I was told they refry their beans in pig lard.

As a vegetarian I am disgusted that they would do this. Why name something vegetarian and comfirm its vegitarian if it is not.

I have no doubt but their food is probably good since they have good ratings but I just wanted to let the future vegetarians know the BEANS contain PIG LARD.

Vegetarian; a person who does not eat meat, and sometimes other animal products, especially for moral, religious, or health reasons.< /review>

< text>
If I could rate this dealership has zero I would. I know that salesman are sometimes a little Sleazy and who sell their soul just to make a sale I have never in my life been treated with such disrespect, blatant disrespect. Nor have I ever seen anybody willing to take advantage of an elderly couple the way that Jeff has. There were other salesmen and finance managers involved however Jeff was the root  the disrespect and complete deception. Thanks to the staff at Swanson fahrney Ford my elderly parents who suffer who suffer from dementia and are constantly under the influence of prescription medications and not able to make sound judgement nor sign contracts, purchase a vehicle that is a piece of junk and that they cannot afford. I pray that I'm able to assist financially enough to prevent the damage that Jeff has possibly done to my parents. When I called to discuss this issue they ask for my mother's permission to talk to me, she gave permission. I explained what the issue was to Ozzy the finance manager who said that he would take it to the owner mr. Fahrney himself. The next message that I got was later that night when I had asked my mom if anybody had called and she told me, "oh yes they did call and tell me that they cannot talk to you because you are not on the contract". So even though my mother gave permission but them to speak to me, they refused my calls because they know that they did wrong and they know that I was not going to stop until they made it right and they didn't want to lose that sale. If you value your family and your bank account, don't buy Swanson fahrney Ford. Had it not been for my father being so upset and grief-stricken begging me to Let It Go so that we can figure out how to move forward, I would have been fighting a lot harder for this but unfortunately respected my father's wishes. Today was a different day he decided he wanted to fight but instead of them talking to my parents he waited and talk to me separately and not nicely either I reminded Jeff that coercion was illegal in many instances and he simply said he didn't understand. Yes when you manipulate the situation and convince an innocent party to buy something that you know is not good for them, especially when you were asked face-to-face by their caregiver to call her if they happened to come back and you refuse to do so, that is a form of coercion as well as a display of many other horrible morals. Lastly and not even half as important as the damage that they've done to an innocent elderly couple, they let them leave with a filthy car and when we brought back today to have it detailed and left almost as filthy and with extra scratches on the dash. Just vacuumed a bit and rinsed the dust off. I guess I still thought there were decent salesman around since I had such a wonderful experience recently (at carmax) but that was my mistake for assuming. This post and these pictures are 1.5 hours after leaving swanson fahrney ford. No extra trips, just brought them home to rest.< /text>

< Review>
I have not purchased a car from Swanson Fahrney, and at this point am not likely to. But my beef is with the service department. My last service, I had a number of routine maintenance items taken care of as well as rear brake replacement.  I am in the habit of taking my own oil in because I have used synthetic oil in my 2007 Rav4 since it was new, and it can be purchased for much less at Costco. They have changed my oil over the years a number of times, and on about 3 occasion the tech has failed to use my oil. This is particularly irritating as I then pay for a lower grade of oil that I do not want, and end up with my own oil sitting there. Yet, I've always returned.
This time my bill was just under $1,300.00. Left the car there for two and a half days. When I pick it up, they have washed the exterior, but done nothing on the interior. Now that's a complimentary service, so it doesn't get done, no big deal. I do rather dislike that the service order says they did it when, in fact, they did not.
Next issue: My oil sits unused. Been there done that.
Next issue: The form where they inspect the car is only partially filled out and very haphazard.  For instance, it would have been nice to know what the state of wear on my front brakes is, but they didn't bother to check it, or, at least didn't bother to put it on the form.  Also, no tire tread figure, nor check of the spare tire inflation pressure.
Then the sticker on the windshield that is supposed to indicate when it is time to return the car for the next oil change, has a mileage which is already passed as the time to return. Sloppy, sloppy, sloppy. For this I leave the car two and a half days, and pay $1,300.00.
To add insult to injury, there is a note that says if you are not happy with the service, please call the service manager, Mr. Michael Mankin. I called him, and was told he was in a meeting. They took my number and said he would call back.  A week later and no call back. So I call again. I was very polite, not angry and not asking for anything. He said he would check out my issues and get back to me that day. Surprise! No call back.
So, after years of dealing with Swanson-Fahrney, I shall be looking for a new service provider.</Review>
